\subsection{Detailed Description}
This group contains public definitions and functions providing access to the GS2000's SPI.

\label{a00655_ga1399b803d30956e8ed6f4929033329ad}


Gsn SPI serial Clock Phase types. 

This Enum defines the phase of the serial clock determining the relationship of the serial clock and the slave select signal. Data is either captured on the first toggling edge of the serial clock (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0) or the second edge (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180) after the falling edge of slave select signal. The field is only valid for Motorola SPI protocol GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0 -\/ serial clock toggles in middle of first data bit GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180-\/ serial clock toggles at start of first data bit

This enum defines SPI clock phase. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00655_ga1399b803d30956e8ed6f4929033329ad}{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE\_\-T}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\label{a00655_ga40c914db809ec79fd3a564dda8364aea}


Gsn SPI clock polarity types. 

This enum defines SPI clock polarity of the inactive serial clock The field is only valid for Motorola SPI protocol. GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-POL\_\-ACTIVELOW -\/ Inactive state of serial clock is low GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-POL\_\-ACTIVEHIGH -\/ Inactive state of serial clock is high

Gsn SPI data word size types. 

This Enum defines the size of data words to be used for next transfer. If the data word size is a sub-\/multiple of the FIFO size it is possible to transfer multiple words per FIFO location. GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-4 4 bit to GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-16 16 bit

\hypertarget{a00655_gad25e484c9005210b7db2528764be5034}{
\index{GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}!GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE@{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE}}
\index{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE@{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE}!GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}}
\subsubsection[{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE}}}
\label{a00655_gad25e484c9005210b7db2528764be5034}


Gsn SPI serial Clock Phase types. 

This Enum defines the phase of the serial clock determining the relationship of the serial clock and the slave select signal. Data is either captured on the first toggling edge of the serial clock (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0) or the second edge (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180) after the falling edge of slave select signal. The field is only valid for Motorola SPI protocol GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0 -\/ serial clock toggles in middle of first data bit GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180-\/ serial clock toggles at start of first data bit

This enum defines SPI clock phase. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00655_ga1399b803d30956e8ed6f4929033329ad}{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE\_\-T}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Gsn SPI data word size types. 

This Enum defines the size of data words to be used for next transfer. If the data word size is a sub-\/multiple of the FIFO size it is possible to transfer multiple words per FIFO location. GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-4 4 bit to GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-16 16 bit

\label{a00655_gae764e5eefaf1dedaf1561a7cd3ccb6aa}


Gsn SPI serial Clock Phase types. 

This Enum defines the phase of the serial clock determining the relationship of the serial clock and the slave select signal. Data is either captured on the first toggling edge of the serial clock (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0) or the second edge (GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180) after the falling edge of slave select signal. The field is only valid for Motorola SPI protocol GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0 -\/ serial clock toggles in middle of first data bit GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-180-\/ serial clock toggles at start of first data bit

This enum defines SPI clock phase. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{a00655_ga1399b803d30956e8ed6f4929033329ad}{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CLOCKPHASE\_\-T}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{Desc}
\item[Enumerator: ]\par
\begin{description}
\index{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-FS\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0@{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-FS\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0}!GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}}\index{GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}!GSN\_\-SPI\_\-FS\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0@{GSN\_\-SPI\_\-FS\_\-CLK\_\-PHASE\_\-0}}\item[{\em

Gsn SPI data word size types. 

This Enum defines the size of data words to be used for next transfer. If the data word size is a sub-\/multiple of the FIFO size it is possible to transfer multiple words per FIFO location. GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-4 4 bit to GSN\_\-SPI\_\-DATAWORDSIZE\_\-16 16 bit

\item[{{\bf GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T} $\ast$}]{spiRW}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}
\label{a00655_ga29d51974bb0e80ae4191a339731c3319}


SPI Read and write through specified port in master mode. 

This function transfers data in master mode. It checks for transfer possibility and then prepares for data transfer. It takes two parameters; one is a valid handle pointer and other is a data pointer of structure GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T. In case of a synchronous call, it returns after data transfer is complete. In case of a asynchronous call, it returns without waiting for data transfer. The callback function specified in pSpiRW(GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T) is called after data transfer is complete.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em spiHandle} & -\/ IN pointer to handle. \\
\hline
{\em spiRW} & -\/ INOUT pointer to hold read and write data pointers and data length. It also holds callback function pointers.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-FAILURE If data pointer is NULL 

GSN\_\-SPI\_\-BUSY If data transfer is running 

GSN\_\-SUCCESS Operation is successful 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{a00655_ga979f498b435e07948e147f852955d792}{

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}
\label{a00655_ga5733034f9b6e7a4307c9a42ae94ff331}


SPI Read and write through specified port in slave mode. 

This function allows transferring data in slave mode. It waits for external clock. It checks for transfer availability and then prepares for data transfer. It accepts two parameters; one is a valid handle pointer and other is data pointer of the structure GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T. In case of a synchronous call, it returns after the data transfer done. In case of an asynchronous call, it returns without waiting for data transfer. The call back function specified in pSpiRW(GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T) is called after data transfer complete. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em spiHandle} & -\/ IN pointer to handle. \\
\hline
{\em spiRW} & -\/ INOUT pointer to hold read write data pointer and data length. Also holds callback function pointers.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-FAILURE If data pointer is NULL 

GSN\_\-SPI\_\-BUSY If data transfer is running 

GSN\_\-SUCCESS Operation is successful 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{a00655_ga687e89dafd17ddd4cc90c4b744e3696d}{

SPI Driver open. 

This function initializes the specified SPI port, with required configuration parameters provided in GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CONFIG\_\-T. This function also initializes the pointer \char`\"{}spiHandle \char`\"{} and creates the synchronous semaphore. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em spiPortNumber} & -\/ IN SPI port number. see GSN\_\-SPI\_\-NUM\_\-T \\

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-SUCCESS -\/ Initialization successful. 

GSN\_\-FAILURE -\/ Initialization failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}
\label{a00655_gad34396a6807c38a140af6fbf0cdd1bc4}


SPI Read and write through specified port in slave mode. 

This function allows transferring data in slave mode. It waits for external clock. It checks for transfer availability and then prepares for data transfer. It accepts two parameters; one is a valid handle pointer and other is data pointer of the structure GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T. In case of a synchronous call, it returns after the data transfer done. In case of an asynchronous call, it returns without waiting for data transfer. The call back function specified in pSpiRW(GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T) is called after data transfer complete.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em spiHandle} & -\/ IN pointer to handle. \\
\hline
{\em spiRW} & -\/ INOUT pointer to hold read write data pointer and data length. Also holds callback function pointers.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-FAILURE If data pointer is NULL 

GSN\_\-SPI\_\-BUSY If data transfer is running 

GSN\_\-SUCCESS Operation is successful 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{a00655_ga08002b3f127d297a7cf861236e16b5d2}{
\index{GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}!GsnSpiFS\_\-SlaveWrite@{GsnSpiFS\_\-SlaveWrite}}

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{a00655_ga92f3c7ce5633d6ae76f1d37062716676}{
\index{GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}!GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite@{GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite}}
\index{GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite@{GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite}!GSN SPI API@{GSN SPI API}}
\subsubsection[{GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}PUBLIC {\bf GSN\_\-STATUS} GsnSpiPoll\_\-MasterReadWrite (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf GSN\_\-SPI\_\-HANDLE\_\-T} $\ast$}]{spiHandle, }
\item[{{\bf GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T} $\ast$}]{spiRW}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}
\label{a00655_ga92f3c7ce5633d6ae76f1d37062716676}


Polling method SPI Read and write through specified port in master mode. 

This function Write and read data in master mode using polling method. It takes two parameters; one is a valid handle pointer and other is a data pointer of structure GSN\_\-SPI\_\-RW\_\-ARGS\_\-T. There is no callbacks hence callbacks are NULL.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em spiHandle} & -\/ IN pointer to handle. \\
\hline
{\em spiRW} & -\/ INOUT pointer to hold read and write data pointers and data length.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-FAILURE If data pointer is NULL 

GSN\_\-SUCCESS Operation is successful 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Polling SPI Driver open. 

This function initializes the specified SPI port in polling mode, with required configuration parameters provided in GSN\_\-SPI\_\-CONFIG\_\-T. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em spiHandle} & -\/ IN pointer to handle. \\
\hline
{\em spiPortNumber} & -\/ IN SPI port number. see GSN\_\-SPI\_\-NUM\_\-T \\
\hline
{\em gsnSpiConfig} & -\/ IN SPI port configuration\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
GSN\_\-SUCCESS -\/ Initialization successful. 

GSN\_\-FAILURE -\/ Initialization failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
